\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{    What is this?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{    \string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{    olc::PixelGameEngine is a single file, cross platform graphics and userinput}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{    framework used for games, visualisations, algorithm exploration and learning.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{    It was developed by YouTuber "{}javidx9"{} as an assistive tool for many of his}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{    videos. The goal of this project is to provide high speed graphics with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{    minimal project setup complexity, to encourage new programmers, younger people,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{    and anyone else that wants to make fun things.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{    However, olc::PixelGameEngine is not a toy! It is a powerful and fast utility}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{    capable of delivering high resolution, high speed, high quality applications}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{    which behave the same way regardless of the operating system or platform.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{    This file provides the core utility set of the olc::PixelGameEngine, including}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{    window creation, keyboard/mouse input, main game thread, timing, pixel drawing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{    routines, image/sprite loading and drawing routines, and a bunch of utility}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{    types to make rapid development of games/visualisations possible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{73 \textcolor{comment}{    Compiling in Linux}}
\DoxyCodeLine{74 \textcolor{comment}{    \string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~}}
\DoxyCodeLine{75 \textcolor{comment}{    You will need a modern C++ compiler, so update yours!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{76 \textcolor{comment}{    To compile use the command:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{77 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{78 \textcolor{comment}{    g++ -\/o YourProgName YourSource.cpp -\/lX11 -\/lGL -\/lpthread -\/lpng -\/lstdc++fs -\/std=c++17}}
\DoxyCodeLine{79 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{80 \textcolor{comment}{    On some Linux configurations, the frame rate is locked to the refresh}}
\DoxyCodeLine{81 \textcolor{comment}{    rate of the monitor. This engine tries to unlock it but may not be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{82 \textcolor{comment}{    able to, in which case try launching your program like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{83 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{84 \textcolor{comment}{    vblank\_mode=0 ./YourProgName}}
\DoxyCodeLine{85 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{87 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{88 \textcolor{comment}{    Compiling in Code::Blocks on Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{89 \textcolor{comment}{    \string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90 \textcolor{comment}{    Well I wont judge you, but make sure your Code::Blocks installation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{91 \textcolor{comment}{    is really up to date -\/ you may even consider updating your C++ toolchain}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92 \textcolor{comment}{    to use MinGW32-\/W64.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94 \textcolor{comment}{    Guide for installing recent GCC for Windows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{95 \textcolor{comment}{    https://www.msys2.org/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{96 \textcolor{comment}{    Guide for configuring code::blocks:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97 \textcolor{comment}{    https://solarianprogrammer.com/2019/11/05/install-\/gcc-\/windows/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 \textcolor{comment}{    https://solarianprogrammer.com/2019/11/16/install-\/codeblocks-\/gcc-\/windows-\/build-\/c-\/cpp-\/fortran-\/programs/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{99 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100 \textcolor{comment}{    Add these libraries to "{}Linker Options"{}:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{101 \textcolor{comment}{    user32 gdi32 opengl32 gdiplus Shlwapi dwmapi stdc++fs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{comment}{    Set these compiler options: -\/std=c++17}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107 \textcolor{comment}{    Compiling on Mac -\/ EXPERIMENTAL! PROBABLY HAS BUGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108 \textcolor{comment}{    \string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \textcolor{comment}{    Yes yes, people use Macs for C++ programming! Who knew? Anyway, enough}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110 \textcolor{comment}{    arguing, thanks to Mumflr the PGE is now supported on Mac. Now I know nothing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111 \textcolor{comment}{    about Mac, so if you need support, I suggest checking out the instructions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112 \textcolor{comment}{    here: https://github.com/MumflrFumperdink/olcPGEMac}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{114 \textcolor{comment}{    clang++ -\/arch x86\_64 -\/std=c++17 -\/mmacosx-\/version-\/min=10.15 -\/Wall -\/framework OpenGL }}
\DoxyCodeLine{115 \textcolor{comment}{        -\/framework GLUT -\/framework Carbon -\/lpng YourSource.cpp -\/o YourProgName}}
\DoxyCodeLine{116 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{117 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{118 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{119 \textcolor{comment}{    Compiling with Emscripten (New \& Experimental)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{120 \textcolor{comment}{    \string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~}}
\DoxyCodeLine{121 \textcolor{comment}{    Emscripten compiler will turn your awesome C++ PixelGameEngine project into WASM!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{122 \textcolor{comment}{    This means you can run your application in teh browser, great for distributing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{123 \textcolor{comment}{    and submission in to jams and things! It's a bit new at the moment. }}
\DoxyCodeLine{124 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{125 \textcolor{comment}{    em++ -\/std=c++17 -\/O2 -\/s ALLOW\_MEMORY\_GROWTH=1 -\/s MAX\_WEBGL\_VERSION=2 -\/s MIN\_WEBGL\_VERSION=2 -\/s USE\_LIBPNG=1 ./YourSource.cpp -\/o pge.html}}
\DoxyCodeLine{126 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{    Using stb\_image.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{comment}{    \string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{comment}{    The PGE will load png images by default (with help from libpng on non-\/windows systems).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{comment}{    However, the excellent "{}stb\_image.h"{} can be used instead, supporting a variety of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{comment}{    image formats, and has no library dependence -\/ something we like at OLC studios ;)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{comment}{    To use stb\_image.h, make sure it's in your code base, and simply:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{comment}{    \#define OLC\_IMAGE\_STB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{comment}{    Before including the olcPixelGameEngine.h header file. stb\_image.h works on many systems}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 \textcolor{comment}{    and can be downloaded here: https://github.com/nothings/stb/blob/master/stb\_image.h}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 \textcolor{comment}{    Multiple cpp file projects?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{144 \textcolor{comment}{    \string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~\string~}}
\DoxyCodeLine{145 \textcolor{comment}{    As a single header solution, the OLC\_PGE\_APPLICATION definition is used to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{146 \textcolor{comment}{    insert the engine implementation at a project location of your choosing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{    The simplest way to setup multifile projects is to create a file called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{    "{}olcPixelGameEngine.cpp"{} which includes the following:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{149 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{150 \textcolor{comment}{    \#define OLC\_PGE\_APPLICATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{    \#include "{}olcPixelGameEngine.h"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{152 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{153 \textcolor{comment}{    That's all it should include. You can also include PGEX includes and }}
\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{    defines in here too. With this in place, you dont need to }}
\DoxyCodeLine{155 \textcolor{comment}{    \#define OLC\_PGE\_APPLICATION anywhere, and can simply include this }}
\DoxyCodeLine{156 \textcolor{comment}{    header file as an when you need to.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{157 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{158 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{159 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{160 \textcolor{comment}{    Ports}}

\DoxyCodeLine{163 \textcolor{comment}{    success to: WinXP, Win7, Win8, Win10, Various Linux, Raspberry Pi,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{164 \textcolor{comment}{    Chromebook, Playstation Portable (PSP) and Nintendo Switch. If you are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{165 \textcolor{comment}{    interested in the details of these ports, come and visit the Discord!}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1336     Pixel Sprite::SampleBL(\textcolor{keywordtype}{float} u, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v)\textcolor{keyword}{ const}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1337 \textcolor{keyword}{    }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1338         u = u * width -\/ 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1339         v = v * height -\/ 0.5f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1340         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x = (int)floor(u); \textcolor{comment}{// cast to int rounds toward zero, not downward}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1341         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y = (int)floor(v); \textcolor{comment}{// Thanks @joshinils}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1342         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} u\_ratio = u -\/ x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1343         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_ratio = v -\/ y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1344         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} u\_opposite = 1 -\/ u\_ratio;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1345         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_opposite = 1 -\/ v\_ratio;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1346 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1347         \mbox{\hyperlink{structolc_1_1_pixel}{olc::Pixel}} p1 = GetPixel(std::max(x, 0), std::max(y, 0));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1348         \mbox{\hyperlink{structolc_1_1_pixel}{olc::Pixel}} p2 = GetPixel(std::min(x + 1, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})width -\/ 1), std::max(y, 0));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1349         \mbox{\hyperlink{structolc_1_1_pixel}{olc::Pixel}} p3 = GetPixel(std::max(x, 0), std::min(y + 1, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})height -\/ 1));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1350         \mbox{\hyperlink{structolc_1_1_pixel}{olc::Pixel}} p4 = GetPixel(std::min(x + 1, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})width -\/ 1), std::min(y + 1, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})height -\/ 1));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1351 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1352         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \mbox{\hyperlink{structolc_1_1_pixel}{olc::Pixel}}(}

\DoxyCodeLine{1488     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} ResourcePack::LoadPack(\textcolor{keyword}{const} std::string\& sFile, \textcolor{keyword}{const} std::string\& sKey)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1489     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1490         \textcolor{comment}{// Open the resource file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1491         baseFile.open(sFile, std::ifstream::binary);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1492         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!baseFile.is\_open()) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1493 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1494         \textcolor{comment}{// 1) Read Scrambled index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1495         uint32\_t nIndexSize = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1496         baseFile.read((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nIndexSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1497 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1498         std::vector<char> buffer(nIndexSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1499         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t j = 0; j < nIndexSize; j++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1500             buffer[j] = baseFile.get();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1501 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1502         std::vector<char> decoded = scramble(buffer, sKey);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1503         \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} pos = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1504         \textcolor{keyword}{auto} read = [\&decoded, \&pos](\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* dst, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} size) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1505             memcpy((\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)dst, (\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)(decoded.data() + pos), size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1506             pos += size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1507         \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1508 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1509         \textcolor{keyword}{auto} get = [\&read]() -\/> \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \{ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c; read(\&c, 1); \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c; \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1510 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1511         \textcolor{comment}{// 2) Read Map}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1512         uint32\_t nMapEntries = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1513         read((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nMapEntries, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1514         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t i = 0; i < nMapEntries; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1515         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1516             uint32\_t nFilePathSize = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1517             read((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nFilePathSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1518 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1519             std::string sFileName(nFilePathSize, \textcolor{charliteral}{' '});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1520             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t j = 0; j < nFilePathSize; j++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1521                 sFileName[j] = get();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1522 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1523             sResourceFile e;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1524             read((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&e.nSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1525             read((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&e.nOffset, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1526             mapFiles[sFileName] = e;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1527         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1528 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1529         \textcolor{comment}{// Don't close base file! we will provide a stream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1530         \textcolor{comment}{// pointer when the file is requested}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1531         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1532     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1534     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} ResourcePack::SavePack(\textcolor{keyword}{const} std::string\& sFile, \textcolor{keyword}{const} std::string\& sKey)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1535     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1536         \textcolor{comment}{// Create/Overwrite the resource file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1537         std::ofstream ofs(sFile, std::ofstream::binary);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1538         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!ofs.is\_open()) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1539 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1540         \textcolor{comment}{// Iterate through map}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1541         uint32\_t nIndexSize = 0; \textcolor{comment}{// Unknown for now}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1542         ofs.write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nIndexSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1543         uint32\_t nMapSize = uint32\_t(mapFiles.size());}
\DoxyCodeLine{1544         ofs.write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nMapSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1545         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& e : mapFiles)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1546         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1547             \textcolor{comment}{// Write the path of the file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1548             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} nPathSize = e.first.size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1549             ofs.write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nPathSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1550             ofs.write(e.first.c\_str(), nPathSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1551 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1552             \textcolor{comment}{// Write the file entry properties}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1553             ofs.write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&e.second.nSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1554             ofs.write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&e.second.nOffset, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1555         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1556 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1557         \textcolor{comment}{// 2) Write the individual Data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1558         std::streampos offset = ofs.tellp();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1559         nIndexSize = (uint32\_t)offset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1560         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& e : mapFiles)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1561         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1562             \textcolor{comment}{// Store beginning of file offset within resource pack file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1563             e.second.nOffset = (uint32\_t)offset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1564 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1565             \textcolor{comment}{// Load the file to be added}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1566             std::vector<uint8\_t> vBuffer(e.second.nSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1567             std::ifstream i(e.first, std::ifstream::binary);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1568             i.read((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)vBuffer.data(), e.second.nSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1569             i.close();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1570 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1571             \textcolor{comment}{// Write the loaded file into resource pack file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1572             ofs.write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)vBuffer.data(), e.second.nSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1573             offset += e.second.nSize;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1574         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1575 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1576         \textcolor{comment}{// 3) Scramble Index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1577         std::vector<char> stream;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1578         \textcolor{keyword}{auto} write = [\&stream](\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* data, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} size) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1579             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} sizeNow = stream.size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1580             stream.resize(sizeNow + size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1581             memcpy(stream.data() + sizeNow, data, size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1582         \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1583 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1584         \textcolor{comment}{// Iterate through map}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1585         write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nMapSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1586         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& e : mapFiles)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1587         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1588             \textcolor{comment}{// Write the path of the file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1589             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} nPathSize = e.first.size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1590             write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nPathSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1591             write(e.first.c\_str(), nPathSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1592 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1593             \textcolor{comment}{// Write the file entry properties}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1594             write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&e.second.nSize, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1595             write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&e.second.nOffset, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1596         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1597         std::vector<char> sIndexString = scramble(stream, sKey);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1598         uint32\_t nIndexStringLen = uint32\_t(sIndexString.size());}
\DoxyCodeLine{1599         \textcolor{comment}{// 4) Rewrite Map (it has been updated with offsets now)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1600         \textcolor{comment}{// at start of file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1601         ofs.seekp(0, std::ios::beg);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1602         ofs.write((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)\&nIndexStringLen, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(uint32\_t));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1603         ofs.write(sIndexString.data(), nIndexStringLen);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1604         ofs.close();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1605         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1606     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1614     std::vector<char> ResourcePack::scramble(\textcolor{keyword}{const} std::vector<char>\& data, \textcolor{keyword}{const} std::string\& key)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1615     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1616         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (key.empty()) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1617         std::vector<char> o;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1619         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keyword}{auto} s : data) o.push\_back(s \string^ key[(c++) \% key.size()]);}

\DoxyCodeLine{1827     \textcolor{comment}{// This is it, the critical function that plots a pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1828     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} PixelGameEngine::Draw(int32\_t x, int32\_t y, Pixel p)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1829     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1830         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!pDrawTarget) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1831 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1832         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (nPixelMode == Pixel::NORMAL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1833         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1834             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} pDrawTarget-\/>SetPixel(x, y, p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1835         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1836 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1837         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (nPixelMode == Pixel::MASK)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1839             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (p.a == 255)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1840                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} pDrawTarget-\/>SetPixel(x, y, p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1841         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1842 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1843         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (nPixelMode == Pixel::ALPHA)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1844         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1845             Pixel d = pDrawTarget-\/>GetPixel(x, y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1846             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} a = (float)(p.a / 255.0f) * fBlendFactor;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1847             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} c = 1.0f -\/ a;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1848             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} r = a * (float)p.r + c * (\textcolor{keywordtype}{float})d.r;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1849             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} g = a * (float)p.g + c * (\textcolor{keywordtype}{float})d.g;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1850             \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} b = a * (float)p.b + c * (\textcolor{keywordtype}{float})d.b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1851             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} pDrawTarget-\/>SetPixel(x, y, Pixel((uint8\_t)r, (uint8\_t)g, (uint8\_t)b\textcolor{comment}{/*, (uint8\_t)(p.a * fBlendFactor)*/}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1852         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1853 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1854         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (nPixelMode == Pixel::CUSTOM)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1855         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1856             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} pDrawTarget-\/>SetPixel(x, y, funcPixelMode(x, y, p, pDrawTarget-\/>GetPixel(x, y)));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1857         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1858 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1859         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1860     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1862 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1863     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} PixelGameEngine::DrawLine(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structolc_1_1v2d__generic}{olc::vi2d}}\& pos1, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structolc_1_1v2d__generic}{olc::vi2d}}\& pos2, Pixel p, uint32\_t pattern)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1864     \{ DrawLine(pos1.x, pos1.y, pos2.x, pos2.y, p, pattern); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1865 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1866     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} PixelGameEngine::DrawLine(int32\_t x1, int32\_t y1, int32\_t x2, int32\_t y2, Pixel p, uint32\_t pattern)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1867     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1868         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x, y, dx, dy, dx1, dy1, px, py, xe, ye, i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1869         dx = x2 -\/ x1; dy = y2 -\/ y1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1870 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1871         \textcolor{keyword}{auto} rol = [\&](void) \{ pattern = (pattern << 1) | (pattern >> 31); \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} pattern \& 1; \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1872 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1873         \textcolor{comment}{// straight lines idea by gurkanctn}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1874         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dx == 0) \textcolor{comment}{// Line is vertical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1875         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1876             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (y2 < y1) std::swap(y1, y2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1877             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (y = y1; y <= y2; y++) \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rol()) Draw(x1, y, p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1878             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1879         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1880 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1881         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dy == 0) \textcolor{comment}{// Line is horizontal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1882         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1883             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (x2 < x1) std::swap(x1, x2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1884             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (x = x1; x <= x2; x++) \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rol()) Draw(x, y1, p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1885             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1886         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1887 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1888         \textcolor{comment}{// Line is Funk-\/aye}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1889         dx1 = abs(dx); dy1 = abs(dy);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1890         px = 2 * dy1 -\/ dx1; py = 2 * dx1 -\/ dy1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1891         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dy1 <= dx1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1892         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1893             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dx >= 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1894             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1895                 x = x1; y = y1; xe = x2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1896             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1897             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1898             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1899                 x = x2; y = y2; xe = x1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1900             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1901 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1902             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rol()) Draw(x, y, p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1903 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1904             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; x < xe; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1905             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1906                 x = x + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1907                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (px < 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1908                     px = px + 2 * dy1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1909                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1910                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1911                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((dx < 0 \&\& dy < 0) || (dx > 0 \&\& dy > 0)) y = y + 1; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} y = y -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1912                     px = px + 2 * (dy1 -\/ dx1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1913                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1914                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rol()) Draw(x, y, p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1915             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1916         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1917         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1918         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1919             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dy >= 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1920             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1921                 x = x1; y = y1; ye = y2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1922             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1923             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1924             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1925                 x = x2; y = y2; ye = y1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1926             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1927 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1928             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rol()) Draw(x, y, p);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1929 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1930             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; y < ye; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1931             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1932                 y = y + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1933                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (py <= 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1934                     py = py + 2 * dx1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1935                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1936                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1937                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((dx < 0 \&\& dy < 0) || (dx > 0 \&\& dy > 0)) x = x + 1; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} x = x -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1938                     py = py + 2 * (dx1 -\/ dy1);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1939                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2667             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'}) \{ pos.y++;  pos.x = 0; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2668             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} pos.x++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2669             size.x = std::max(size.x, pos.x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2670             size.y = std::max(size.y, pos.y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2671         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2672         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} size * 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2673     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2674 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2679     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2680         int32\_t sx = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2681         int32\_t sy = 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2686             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (col.a != 255)       SetPixelMode(Pixel::ALPHA);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2687             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}                    SetPixelMode(Pixel::MASK);}

\DoxyCodeLine{2689         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keyword}{auto} c : sText)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2690         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2691             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{2692             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2693                 sx = 0; sy += 8 * scale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2694             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2695             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2696             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2697                 int32\_t ox = (c -\/ 32) \% 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2698                 int32\_t oy = (c -\/ 32) / 16;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2699 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2700                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (scale > 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2701                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2702                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t i = 0; i < 8; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2703                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t j = 0; j < 8; j++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2704                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fontSprite-\/>GetPixel(i + ox * 8, j + oy * 8).r > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2705                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t is = 0; is < scale; is++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2706                                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t js = 0; js < scale; js++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2707                                         Draw(x + sx + (i * scale) + is, y + sy + (j * scale) + js, col);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2708                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2709                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2710                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2711                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t i = 0; i < 8; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2712                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t j = 0; j < 8; j++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2713                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fontSprite-\/>GetPixel(i + ox * 8, j + oy * 8).r > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2714                                 Draw(x + sx + i, y + sy + j, col);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2715                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2716                 sx += 8 * scale;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2717             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2718         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2719         SetPixelMode(m);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2720     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2721 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2722     \mbox{\hyperlink{structolc_1_1v2d__generic}{olc::vi2d}} PixelGameEngine::GetTextSizeProp(\textcolor{keyword}{const} std::string\& s)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2817     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} PixelGameEngine::olc\_UpdateViewport()}
\DoxyCodeLine{2818     \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2820         int32\_t wh = vScreenSize.y * vPixelSize.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2821         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} wasp = (float)ww / (\textcolor{keywordtype}{float})wh;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2824         \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2830             vViewSize.x = (int32\_t)vWindowSize.x;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2838         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2890     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} PixelGameEngine::EngineThread()}
\DoxyCodeLine{2891     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2892         \textcolor{comment}{// Allow platform to do stuff here if needed, since its now in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2893         \textcolor{comment}{// context of this thread}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2902         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\& ext : vExtensions) ext-\/>OnAfterUserCreate();}

\DoxyCodeLine{2908 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2911             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912                 \textcolor{comment}{// User denied destroy for some reason, so continue running}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913                 bAtomActive = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2939     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} PixelGameEngine::olc\_CoreUpdate()}
\DoxyCodeLine{2940     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2941         \textcolor{comment}{// Handle Timing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2942         m\_tp2 = std::chrono::system\_clock::now();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2943         std::chrono::duration<float> elapsedTime = m\_tp2 -\/ m\_tp1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2944         m\_tp1 = m\_tp2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2945 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2946         \textcolor{comment}{// Our time per frame coefficient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2947         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} fElapsedTime = elapsedTime.count();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2948         fLastElapsed = fElapsedTime;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2949 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2950         \textcolor{comment}{// Some platforms will need to check for events}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2951         platform-\/>HandleSystemEvent();}
\DoxyCodeLine{2952 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2953         \textcolor{comment}{// Compare hardware input states from previous frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2954         \textcolor{keyword}{auto} ScanHardware = [\&](HWButton* pKeys, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}* pStateOld, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}* pStateNew, uint32\_t nKeyCount)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2955         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2956             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (uint32\_t i = 0; i < nKeyCount; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{2957             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2958                 pKeys[i].bPressed = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2959                 pKeys[i].bReleased = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2960                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pStateNew[i] != pStateOld[i])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2961                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2962                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pStateNew[i])}
\DoxyCodeLine{2963                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2964                         pKeys[i].bPressed = !pKeys[i].bHeld;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2965                         pKeys[i].bHeld = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2966                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2967                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2968                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2969                         pKeys[i].bReleased = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2970                         pKeys[i].bHeld = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2971                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2972                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2973                 pStateOld[i] = pStateNew[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{2974             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2975         \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2976 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2977         ScanHardware(pKeyboardState, pKeyOldState, pKeyNewState, 256);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2978         ScanHardware(pMouseState, pMouseOldState, pMouseNewState, nMouseButtons);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2979 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2980         \textcolor{comment}{// Cache mouse coordinates so they remain consistent during frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2981         vMousePos = vMousePosCache;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2982         nMouseWheelDelta = nMouseWheelDeltaCache;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2983         nMouseWheelDeltaCache = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2984 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2985         \textcolor{comment}{//  renderer-\/>ClearBuffer(olc::BLACK, true);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2986 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2987         \textcolor{comment}{// Handle Frame Update}}

\DoxyCodeLine{4145                 png\_byte bit\_depth;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4146                 png\_bytep* row\_pointers;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4147                 spr-\/>width = png\_get\_image\_width(png, info);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4149                 color\_type = png\_get\_color\_type(png, info);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4150                 bit\_depth = png\_get\_bit\_depth(png, info);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4151                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (bit\_depth == 16) png\_set\_strip\_16(png);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4152                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (color\_type == PNG\_COLOR\_TYPE\_PALETTE) png\_set\_palette\_to\_rgb(png);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4153                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (color\_type == PNG\_COLOR\_TYPE\_GRAY \&\& bit\_depth < 8) png\_set\_expand\_gray\_1\_2\_4\_to\_8(png);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4154                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (png\_get\_valid(png, info, PNG\_INFO\_tRNS)) png\_set\_tRNS\_to\_alpha(png);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4158                     png\_set\_gray\_to\_rgb(png);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4159                 png\_read\_update\_info(png, info);}

\DoxyCodeLine{4183             \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{5202 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5203             \textcolor{comment}{// width / height = aspect ratio}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5204             Module.\_olc\_WindowAspectRatio = \$0 / \$1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5205             Module.canvas.parentNode.addEventListener(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}resize"{}}, \textcolor{keyword}{function}(e) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5206                 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5207                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (e.defaultPrevented) \{ e.stopPropagation();  return; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5208                 var viewWidth = e.detail.width;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5209                 var viewHeight = e.detail.width / Module.\_olc\_WindowAspectRatio;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5210                 if (viewHeight > e.detail.height)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5211                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5212                     viewHeight = e.detail.height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5213                     viewWidth = e.detail.height * Module.\_olc\_WindowAspectRatio;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5214                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5215                     }
\DoxyCodeLine{5216                 if (Module.canvas.parentNode.className == \textcolor{stringliteral}{'emscripten\_border'})}

\DoxyCodeLine{5218 }
